{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01SWcqHw2fnzq3z3CXXdkhrY","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# Building from Source\n     2→\n     3→Pre-built binaries are available for download for a variety of supported platforms through the [HashiCorp Releases website](https://releases.hashicorp.com/terraform/). \n     4→\n     5→However, if you'd like to build Terraform yourself, you can do so using the Go build toolchain and the options specified in this document.\n     6→\n     7→## Prerequisites\n     8→\n     9→1. Ensure you've installed the Go language version specified in [`.go-version`](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/main/.go-version).\n    10→2. Clone this repository to a location of your choice.\n    11→\n    12→## Terraform Build Options\n    13→\n    14→Terraform accepts certain options passed using `ldflags` at build time which control the behavior of the resulting binary.\n    15→\n    16→### Dev Version Reporting\n    17→\n    18→Terraform will include a `-dev` flag when reporting its own version (ex: 1.5.0-dev) unless `version.dev` is set to `no`:\n    19→\n    20→```\n    21→go build -ldflags \"-w -s -X 'github.com/hashicorp/terraform/version.dev=no'\" -o bin/ .\n    22→```\n    23→\n    24→### Experimental Features\n    25→\n    26→Experimental features of Terraform will be disabled unless `main.experimentsAllowed` is set to `yes`:\n    27→\n    28→```\n    29→go build -ldflags \"-w -s -X 'main.experimentsAllowed=yes'\" -o bin/ .\n    30→```\n    31→\n    32→In the official build process for Terraform, experiments are only allowed in alpha release builds. We recommend that third-party distributors follow that convention in order to reduce user confusion.\n    33→\n    34→## Go Options\n    35→\n    36→For the most part, the Terraform release process relies on the Go toolchain defaults for the target operating system and processor architecture.\n    37→\n    38→### `CGO_ENABLED`\n    39→\n    40→One exception is the `CGO_ENABLED` option, which is set explicitly when building Terraform binaries. For most platforms, we build with `CGO_ENABLED=0` in order to produce a statically linked binary. Ensure you've installed the Go language version specified in [`.go-version`](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/main/.go-version).\n2. Clone this repository to a location of your choice.\n\n## Terraform Build Options\n\nTerraform accepts certain options passed using `ldflags` at build time which control the behavior of the resulting binary.\n\n### Dev Version Reporting\n\nTerraform will include a `-dev` flag when reporting its own version (ex: 1.5.0-dev) unless `version.dev` is set to `no`:\n\n```\ngo build -ldflags \"-w -s -X 'github.com/hashicorp/terraform/version.dev=no'\" -o bin/ .\n```\n\n### Experimental Features\n\nExperimental features of Terraform will be disabled unless `main.experimentsAllowed` is set to `yes`:\n\n```\ngo build -ldflags \"-w -s -X 'main.experimentsAllowed=yes'\" -o bin/ .\n```\n\nIn the official build process for Terraform, experiments are only allowed in alpha release builds. We recommend that third-party distributors follow that convention in order to reduce user confusion.\n\n## Go Options\n\nFor the most part, the Terraform release process relies on the Go toolchain defaults for the target operating system and processor architecture.\n\n### `CGO_ENABLED`\n\nOne exception is the `CGO_ENABLED` option, which is set explicitly when building Terraform binaries. \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// these leftRule* variables are markers for the beginning of the lines\n\t// containing the diagnostic that are intended to help sighted users\n\t// better Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/terraform\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact formatted summary of the plan's resource changes.\n// It groups changes by action type and outputs one line per resource change,\n// ending with a summary of the total changes.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != \"\" {\n\t\t\t// Skip deposed resources\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tactionGroups[rc.Action] = append(actionGroups[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order in which to display actions\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort resources within each action group\n\tfor _, resources := range actionGroups {\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\t// Output resources grouped by action\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Only show non-NoOp actions\n\t\tif action != plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"\\n# %s\\n\", actionSymbolAndName(action)))\n\t\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", rc.Addr.String()))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add summary\n\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n# Summary\\n\")\n\tsummary := countChanges(actionGroups)\n\tfor _, text := range summary {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", text))\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolAndName returns a human-readable name for an action.\nfunc actionSymbolAndName(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"[+] Resources to create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"[~] Resources to update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"[-] Resources to delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"[∓] Resources to replace\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"[±] Resources to replace\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"[+.] Resources to create and forget\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"[.] Resources to forget\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"[<=] Resources to read\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"[no change] Resources with no changes\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"[?] Resources with unknown action\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a summary of the changes by action type.\nfunc countChanges(actionGroups map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) []string {\n\tvar summary []string\n\n\tcreateCount := len(actionGroups[plans.Create])\n\tupdateCount := len(actionGroups[plans.Update])\n\tdeleteCount := len(actionGroups[plans.Delete])\n\treplaceCount := len(actionGroups[plans.DeleteThenCreate]) + formatted summary of the plan's resource changes.\n// It groups changes by action type and outputs one line per resource change,\n// ending with a summary of the total changes.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources countChanges(actionGroups)\n\tfor _, text := range summary {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", text))\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolAndName returns a human-readable
